<Rating>2<//Rating>< Review>
I went here to try the Bahn Mi sandwich.
My takeaway was: the cucumber doesn't seem pickled and the tofu is very sweet, and although they say there are jalapenos, there sure don't seem to be, and it ironically has virtually no spice. I consider it very mediocre. If you like authentic veitnamese then you probably would not prefer this.

My other big issue is how the menu is structured with the format: Step 1, Step 2, etc. It turns out that you are not ordering a meal as implied but everything separately. The format realisticly should be: Main, Appetizers, Drinks. Once your done building a meal it's upwards of around $15. A tofu Bahn Mi sandwich alone was $7.63 which is much more then all the other locations I frequent where the prices range from $3.50 - $5 and are more authentic.</Review>

Sean Schluntz< /Name>
< Review>
I lived on Vietnamese sandwiches in college. The fresh crunchy role, the flavorful meat, pickled veggies, and a touch of spice. They were inexpensive so I still had money for beer (um, books.. I mean books).

I don't live those memories here, but I still like to come. The chicken has good flavor, but the pork is bland and kinda soggy. The pickled veggies seem damp and the bread is often a bit soft with little or no crunch. That said the food is still enjoyable.

I've read others say that it's like a fast food version of a Vietnamese shop and I think that is a good description. I've been here a few times now with my wife. We both really enjoy the pork bun and the chips. She's found a bowl she likes and I think this could become a regular stop when we want something fast. I think I'll be sticking with the chicken though.<//Review>

< rating>
5< /rating>
< text>
I have passed by this place a few times and was a bit skeptical to try it. I was put-off by the catch-all phrase, "Asian," in their tag line, "Asian Street Food."

I am glad that I tried them, I will definitely be back.

Here's what I got:
Korean Bowl with Five Spice Chicken and the 64 degree egg
Vietnamese Iced Coffee
$12.10 after tax

I would definitely get the Five Spice Chicken and 64 degree egg again, the chicken was very well seasoned and the egg was a perfect consistency with a rich, velvety yolk. I wish the kimchi fried rice in the bowl had a bit more flavor, but the Korean bbq sauce that they put over everything adds the bit of kick that the rice needs.

In the bowl format, the sauce is only on the top layer so when I was down towards the bottom, I found that it got a little bland.

The Vietnamese Iced Coffee seemed like a bit of an afterthought, the flavor and proportions seemed a bit off. There was not enough condensed milk, it wasn't sweet enough.

Next time I will probably try either the beef or the pork, but will probably still get the Korean bowl. I felt like the egg was well worth the additional $1.25 and will be adding it to all future orders. I will skip the Vietnamese coffee and instead go for Thai iced tea or a water.

In the Vietnamese bowls, if they had gone with vermicelli noodles instead of white rice, I might consider trying that over the Korean bowl.

Overall, their prices are very fair, their food has a well-developed flavor, and they are the perfect walking distance for lunch if you work in Bishop Ranch. This was an easy five stars for me.</text>

<rating>1</rating>< Text>
ER: ZERO STARS. INEPT. INHUMANE. DANGEROUS. DO NOT GO TO THE UCI ER!!!!!

UCI's ER treatment was negligent, inept, careless, and inhumane. Contrast this with the excellent care I received the next day at the Cedars Sinai ER and it's clear UCI's ER has major problems that endanger patients. You do not want yourself or your loved ones to be treated the way this ER treats people.

On August 23rd at 11pm, I was struck with severe abdominal pain while leaving Disneyland. I couldn't stand, and the nurse called for the paramedics who brought me to UCI.

Dr. Deng took my information, then wheeled me into the ER waiting room where I was left, despite the fact that I was visibly shaking in pain. I was left there for a long time, with the worst pain I've ever experienced in the 62-years of my life.

I was literally ignored by the staff as they walked by, even when I called out to them to "please help me, I'm in terrible pain." Nothing. I was finally so scared I called out, "Someone please help me, I'm in pain," to which a woman at the front desk chastised me, "Sir, you need to be quiet."

I was finally admitted and had one good night nurse, Pam. Everyone else acted as if taking care of patients was a bother-- not just me, but the people suffering and moaning in the next curtain on both sides who weren't getting the help they needed.

It took 5 hours for a CT scan

Dr. Xu (a urology resident who I'd never seen before and wouldn't see again) told me I had a kidney stone and that they'd keep me there for the day and if it didn't pass, they'd prep a procedure to remove it.

One hour later I was summarily told I'd been discharged. At this time I was again shaking with pain, I had to go to the bathroom to throw up. When I said I didn't feel well enough to go, I was told that I'd already been discharged. Who made that decision? And how did they do it without ever having seen me? And why would an ER discharge a patient still showing severe symptoms?

Since I had to wait 4 hours to get back to LA, I asked for a single pain pill. They refused. Their pharmacy is closed all weekend!

I was in so much pain I had to go to Cedars Sinai ER the next morning, where they provided excellent care.

Then the UCI ER called to say I had to have a stent removed for a procedure I was never informed of or consented to. Then they weren't sure if I'd had it. WHAT? Nobody at the hospital could tell me. WHAT?

Then my own urologist couldn't get my records from UCI. The timeline they sent me a month later is incomplete and incorrect with substantial gaps.

Frighteningly uncaring incompetence from start to finish.

AND--INCORRECT WRONGFUL BILLING! Billed insurance separately for the CAT scan, which is wrong, it should have been billed under the ER. THEIR mistake lead to a $250 wrongful billing to me. Luckily BlueShield was able to make the correction, but if you get a separate Radiology bill from this horrific ER, call your insurance and get it removed.

(To be clear: I did previously have an excellent experience with a doctor at this facility, so this may be limited to the ER)< /Text>

This is a Shell gas station with a nice little convenience store. The gas was actually cheaper here in Morro Bay than it was in San Luis Obispo.

It has everything you would expect at a service station with a convenience store; beer, snack food, coffee, soft drinks, and things you need on the road.

You need to buy something to use the bathroom, and it is an accessible bathroom.<//Text>

<UserId.>104745753850161072758<//UserId.><user_name>Taylor Johndrew< /user_name><date>1491767213761<//date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
I had a fantastic experience at Urban Glass! Typically, I am very uncomfortable in smoke shops because I don't feel welcome or I feel like I'm wasting the employees time because I am not an expert. I had the exact opposite experience here. James was immediately welcoming, and we had a great conversation. I explained what I wanted, and he showed some pieces at prices I didn't think I could get them for. Other reviews talked about the great prices, and they are 100% true. The shop was small, but had a lot of merchandise for the size. It felt very high end and clean, unlike other shops, and had a great vibe, with cool framed pictures everywhere and shelves made of sick metal pipes and fancy wood. About half of the pieces are locally blown, which is important to me because I like to support local art. I will definitely shop here again!< /Review>

<rate>1<//rate><Text>I have been to noodles and company around the nation. I have been to this particular noodles a couple of times because of the convenience of the location, but I will never return. At noodles the food always is an amazing thrill ride for every single one of my taste buds. I feel as if I can escape reality and take a trip to Italy or Japan etc. depending on what delicious dish I select. Thankfully my taste buds still experienced pure bliss. however the customer service was piss poor. There was one gentleman who was incredibly helpful I believe his name was Chris (and to Chris I give 5 stars) but to the rest of the staff I would give 0 stars if it were possible. Dirty looks were given and smart comments were made as I tried to redeem my rewards from the noodles app, which failed to work. Staff stared and gave dirty looks as I was eating my meal. At the conclusion of my review I would just like to say I love noodles and company and will go back, but I will never go back to the one in San Ramon. < text>
Currently standing waiting for a pick up order. My food is about 10 minutes late. The place is slammed. While most workers seem frustrated and irritable, there is one who stands out, making quick decisions, keeping a cool head, and even when he told me they were out of something I ordered, he was genuinely apologetic and willing to do what he could for me. I think this guys name is Brian or Ryan? Either way, his awesome customer service is the only thing keeping me from being another angry and irritated customer. Keep up the good work! Sorry for the low stars, seems over all the place is understaffed and out of product too early in the day.</text>
